style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4944598\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"722\" style=\"vertical-align: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwb8tgVMUQuHP1hCRfX24n6yWKtlvia4PRHlkcRqISyOft2bwpjmPiabzBg/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">嘉陵江</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">发源于陕西省凤县的秦岭南麓</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">全长1120km，流域面积16万km²</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">是长江水系中<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">流域面积最大</strong>的支流</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">滔滔嘉陵江水，从古至今</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">滋养着<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">广元</strong>、<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">阆中</strong>、<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">南充</strong>等四川东部的主要城市</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">河流一路奔流向南</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">重庆</strong><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">市</strong>朝天门码头汇入长江</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">山高谷深的嘉陵江泥沙含量巨大<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">泥沙淤积会使得河床的高度被抬高<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">而且由于嘉陵江流域的形状略似扇形</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">洪水向中心汇流，加剧涨势<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">常常产生严重的洪灾</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">从1485年到1949年的500年内<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">嘉陵江流域发生洪水<strong>133次</strong>，有<strong>33座县城</strong>遭受洪灾<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">为了治理洪水<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">嘉陵江流域修建了许多水利枢纽进行<strong>调蓄洪水</strong><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如：位于广元市的亭子口水利枢纽<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">以及宝珠寺水电站等<br></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">洪水虽然无情，但是嘉陵江却一直在养育两岸人民<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">嘉陵江沿岸的<strong>水域风光</strong>、<strong>山地景观</strong><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>峡谷森林</strong>都是四川省独一无二的美</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在山势险峻的四川北部地区</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">嘉陵江像一把“利剑”</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">冲破层层山峦的阻碍</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">“劈”开一条险峻地河道</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">正是这条河道</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">拉近了古代陕西和四川人民交流的距离</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"950\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbwolcn6zYm27FVvUtSFAd2hOTw78C0qouS8DpAWvkGfAKAHvhC0ibG0A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: left;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\">剑门关的翠云廊古柏，相传是蜀汉上将张飞所植，至今仍有一万三千余株，上至先秦，历经汉唐，下至明清，不断有人守护着嘉陵江两岸的独特景观</span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">广元，</strong>处在嘉陵江的上游</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">是四川人民出入巴蜀大地的“北大门”</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">从古至今依靠着嘉陵江的庇护</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">世界上最古老、现存最完整的古代交通系统</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">金牛道</strong>即修建在嘉陵江河谷的两侧</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在嘉陵江流域内还分布着</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">陈仓道</strong>、<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">米仓道</strong>和<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">荔枝道</strong>等古蜀道</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"0.66640625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwb1dL67bSopbNtwEpkVGJUPicQjLZ4sGRrlEicLtD3opTiadrDOV8HSrQVw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">蜀道</strong>不仅是蜀国大将姜维镇守蜀国之地<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">更是蜀国与关中乃至中原的重要关系纽带</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">沿着嘉陵江河谷修建的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">金牛道</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">虽然蜿蜒崎岖，但沿途的商贸交流越来越频繁</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">来自蜀国的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">蜀锦</strong>、<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">丝绸</strong>、<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">茶叶</strong>等</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">通过嘉陵江河谷金牛道销往长安</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">中原大地乃至西域各国</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">顾炎武《日知录》中记载：</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">“<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">自秦人取蜀以后，始有茗饮之事</strong>”</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">来自蜀地的粮食与赋税</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">为日后秦统一六国奠定了坚实的基础</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">逐渐地，广元、成都等地的经济开始腾飞</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">到了唐代，成都已成为仅次于扬州的经济发达地区</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">有了“<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">扬一益</strong><strong>二</strong>”的美称</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"0.6671875\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbofdKA9C0ZFbiassOJx83UHfZ3EZTmOxaNwg37gk6srw2esWAlicRdNAA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">不仅上游的经济逐渐繁荣</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">处在下游的重庆市也不甘示弱</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">由于嘉陵江一路南下的过程中</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">“招兵买马”了多条河流</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">特别是在重庆合川区接纳<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">渠江</strong>和<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">涪江</strong>后</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">嘉陵江水量大增</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">两江交汇的重庆自古便是我国内河航运的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">枢纽</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">面对着穿城而过的长江、嘉陵江</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">更是重庆人心中的温暖印记</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">曾经的重庆</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">依靠嘉陵江与长江，实现了<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">内河航运</strong>的兴盛</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如今的重庆</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">长江黄金水道的游轮、货轮往来，又是一派胜景</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">此情此景</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">早已深深地印在重庆人的脑海之中</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">时至今日</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">老重庆人很喜欢在江边走一走</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">每当不开心的时候，来到视野开阔的江边，</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">吹一吹江风，心情就会豁然开朗</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"0.66640625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbd4kaib5kNicTtIKF1FCCeReibVblJ3hftNEUYp4oSKibXEmkicChoMFibeUQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><section style=\"font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 2px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"font-size: 16px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px;background-color: rgba(215, 237, 253, 0.45);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: left;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: -30px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 35px;height: rgb(248, 216, 0) 100%);box-shadow: rgb(255, 190, 39) 0px 0px 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 22px;color: rgba(59, 158, 255, 0.68);line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">2</em></strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-width: 7px 0px 8px;border-radius: 0px 25px 25px;border-style: none none solid;border-color: rgb(112, 188, 240) rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(215, 237, 253);padding: 8px;box-shadow: rgba(0, 135, 227, 0.52) -1.41421px 1.41421px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgba(0, 135, 227, 0.34) 0px 0px 10px inset;border-width: 2px;border-radius: 0px 15px 15px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(255, 251, 247);padding: 10px 15px 10px 25px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"font-size: 17px;color: rgb(0, 135, 227);line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">天府之国的“黄金搭档”—岷江</strong></p></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: right;margin-top: -29px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 57px;height: 30px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4944598\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"722\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwb8tgVMUQuHP1hCRfX24n6yWKtlvia4PRHlkcRqISyOft2bwpjmPiabzBg/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">岷江</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">自北向南贯穿四川省中部的<strong>黄金地带</strong><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">在乐山纳入了<strong>大渡河</strong>和<strong>青衣江</strong>“两员大将”</span></p><p style=\"font-size: 15px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\">最后在<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">宜宾</strong>汇入长江</p><p style=\"font-size: 15px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果说嘉陵江是重庆的命</p><p style=\"font-size: 15px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\">那么岷江则是成都的魂</p><p style=\"font-size: 15px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\">由此可见岷江水系对成都平原有多重要</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></span></p></section></section><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">除了嘉陵江流域，岷江流域是另一个</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">助推成都平原发展的“加速器”<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">巴蜀文明</strong>有近三千年的灿烂与辉煌</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">对于这种文明的来源，说法不一</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">但有很多学者认为</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">早期蜀文化是源于岷江上游的新石器文化</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">着眼全球来看</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">无论是发源于黄河流域的<strong style=\"font-size: 15px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">古代华夏文明</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">发源于两河流域的<span style=\"font-size: 15px;text-align: center;\"></span><span style=\"font-size: 15px;text-align: center;\">古巴比伦文明</span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">发源于尼罗河流域的<span style=\"font-size: 15px;text-align: center;\">古埃及文明</span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">还是发源于恒河流域的<span style=\"font-size: 15px;text-align: center;\">古印度文</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px;text-align: center;\">明</span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">都与江河有着密切的联系</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">而<strong>岷江</strong>自古以来,就是滋润成都平原的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">生命之源</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这里不仅孕育了独特的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">三星堆文明</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">还是许多帝王将相与文人墨客</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">隐居自敛的安适之地</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">既有李商隐“<strong>却话巴山夜雨时</strong>”的温柔<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也有陆游“<strong>细雨骑驴入剑门</strong>”的感慨<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"2.0875\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbqlO4Hor4icZP3MqiaEYyHU4FjS4IU6lM453BpdttMVdayqQ63b9qw33w/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">回顾历史，先人们在开创千年古都的同时</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也开启了中华民族的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">治水先河</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">距今约4000年大禹的治水，正是从岷江开始</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">《尚书·禹贡》记载:“<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">岷山导江,东别为沱</strong>”</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">通过疏导岷江,向东开凿水道治理水害</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">即便如此，岷江的水患灾害还是从未停止</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">汉武帝元封三年（公元前108年）</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">岷江“溢”出，“”漂流万家“</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">据《灌县志》记载，康熙四十五年<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">岷江的支流杂谷脑河在暴雨中<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">“<strong>有二物如牛相斗，山为之崩，横截谷口</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>水不得流者三载。弥漫浸淹</strong></p><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">逆上数十里，官民时惊恐</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">”</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\">由此看来</span></p></section></section><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">岷江给成都平原带来丰富沉积土壤的同时</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">还带来了各种水患灾害</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">直到一千多年后的秦昭王末年</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">蜀郡太守李冰父子修建了<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">都江堰水利枢纽</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">才极大地改善了岷江流域的水患灾害</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">都江堰也是整个岷江流域的“点睛之笔”</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">因为它巧妙地将岷江进行了<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">分流</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">岷江干流在中间</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">干流以北的岷江被分流至成都市区及沱江流域</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">以南的岷江则偏向西南奔流<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在成都西南远郊附近再次汇入岷江</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这么伟大的工程日复一日，年复一年<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">守护着成都平原</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">使成都成为了</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">“<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">水旱从人，食物荒年，不知饥馑</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">天下谓之天府也</strong>”的天府之国</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"1.500441306266549\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1133\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbVIDPPMwfBs5MjIQNpENXpiavM8NcRgDZjLibv3pIrb7CiaHhwbSGiasCJQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><section style=\"font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 2px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"font-size: 16px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 20px;background-color: rgba(215, 237, 253, 0.45);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: left;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: -30px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 35px;height: 35px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 50%;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-image: linear-gradient(135deg, rgb(255, 246, 185) 10%, rgb(248, 216, 0) 100%);box-shadow: rgb(255, 190, 39) 0px 0px 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 22px;color: rgba(59, 158, 255, 0.68);line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">3</em></strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-width: 7px 0px 8px;border-radius: 0px 25px 25px;border-style: none none solid;border-color: rgb(112, 188, 240) rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(215, 237, 253);padding: 8px;box-shadow: rgba(0, 135, 227, 0.52) -1.41421px 1.41421px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgba(0, 135, 227, 0.34) 0px 0px 10px inset;border-width: 2px;border-radius: 0px 15px 15px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(255, 251, 247);padding: 10px 15px 10px 25px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"font-size: 17px;color: rgb(0, 135, 227);line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">天府之国的“另一主力”—沱江</strong></p></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: right;margin-top: -29px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 57px;height: 30px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4944598\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"722\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwb8tgVMUQuHP1hCRfX24n6yWKtlvia4PRHlkcRqISyOft2bwpjmPiabzBg/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">沱江</strong><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">同样是自北向南流</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">流淌了712公里，经过了<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">德阳</strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">资阳</strong>、<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">内江</strong>、<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">自贡</strong>等多个城市后</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">泸州</strong>汇入长江</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">沱江流域面积较小，不像嘉陵江和岷江流域那么广大<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这就使得沱江一旦发生暴雨就会覆盖到全流域<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">1981年7月，沱江上、中游同时发生暴雨</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">干流三皇庙水文站<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">洪峰流量8110立方米每秒<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">超过了历史最大洪水流量<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">面对如此之大的洪水</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">沱江流域同样建起了许多水利枢纽<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">例如：三岔水库和长葫两库等<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在引水灌溉的同时<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">最大程度地调蓄洪水</p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>保证沱江流域及沿岸人民的安全</strong><br></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.4207048\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"454\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbvuTiboyAI1QIkOia3VicY9ZOlgG6uia63EvGicbG9ofObI5HBHtpr5ib2bXg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在沱江流域内</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">生活着<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">1700多万</strong>人，有着<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">1694万亩</strong>的耕地</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">金堂</strong>的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">柑橘</strong><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">，</strong><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">简阳</strong>的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">棉花</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">什邡</strong>的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">烤烟</strong>，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">资阳</strong>的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">花生</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">内江</strong>的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">甘蔗</strong>，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">乐至</strong>的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">蚕桑</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">无论是品质和产量都十分引人注目</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">沱江上游</strong>自古就营种烟叶，什邡、广汉等地的毛烟</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">绵竹的柳烟，很早就声誉鹊起</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">沱江下游</strong>的内江，自古以来就在从事着甜蜜的事业</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">从唐朝开始</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">甘蔗在这个流域中成长壮大</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">手工制糖的作坊自康熙年间兴起后</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">并迅速在沱江两岸扩展开</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">到了光绪末年</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">甘蔗的种植已经扩展到了全省<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">120多个县</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">年产糖品达到<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">7000多万斤</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"1.4705882352941178\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1156\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbxHaSBF7bXrI0PSMTACTSM0JOcJRrSHhzD2jzicibsYUwC74uMOdXHJNA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">处在沱江和长江交汇处的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">泸州</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">更是水的天下</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">若隐若现的酒香，是泸州街头的味道标配</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这里深居巴蜀腹地，气候多雨温和</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">是泸州本地<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">软质小麦</strong>和<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">糯红高粱</strong>的生长乐园</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而这些农作物，正是白酒酿造的上佳原料</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">清代诗人张问陶不禁赞叹道：</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">“<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">衔杯却爱泸州好，十指寒香给客橙</strong>”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">有酒了，怎能少得了肉</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">对于每一座沿江的城市而言</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">鱼都是最受欢迎的，泸州也不例外</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">区别于成渝两地制作的豆瓣沱鱼和干烧鲤鱼</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">泸州当地的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">豆瓣沱鱼</strong>和<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">干烧鲤鱼</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其最大的特点在于使用的是特有的</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">泸州<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">元红豆瓣</strong>以及<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">泸州泡姜</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">更加突出了食物的鲜香和辣味</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6666667\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwb1DWn4h4Q1Mz5X4L3UicKVqSSU4MGVv1yxVJ4fic7tgIuQ7obcUb6uVZw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">泸州泡姜</p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">为了除湿，泸州人将生津润燥的<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">鳝鱼</strong>吃到极致</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">除去内脏后的鳝鱼</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">需要过两遍沸水后捞出</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">随后加入葱、姜、蒜、料酒等作佐料</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">待水煮沸后，把鳝鱼切断后放入沸水中</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">再将火腿片、当归、党参、胡椒粉等注入汤中</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">加盖，用棉纸封口，上笼蒸1小时左右即可</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">出锅后的鳝肉软烂鲜香，汤汁清爽味酽</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6666667\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"600\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/g55FlNiaVwO7p8CM5dzPlFLmLqsATicOwbMPgh7UjyfBnNYIBjRZkrrvxHGqUe59PVr6ibxI5KwuyoN772vyHhsuw/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如此吃，很巴适！</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 0px;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(243, 243, 243);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: -3px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section rgba(223, 46, 0, 0.35);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;align-self: flex-start;flex: 0 0 0%;height: auto;padding-right: 4px;padding-left: 4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section 0.71);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;align-self: flex-start;flex: 0 0 0%;height: auto;padding-right: 4px;padding-left: 4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">从古至今<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: border-box;\">将可能造成的损失降至最低<br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这样才能做到<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">人与自然和谐相处</strong></p></section><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">提到宝石，你能想到哪些？<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">钻石?翡翠？</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">还是“来~左边跟我一起画个龙”？</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">萤石</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">是一种常见的矿物晶体</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">古代的夜明珠便是由萤石制作</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如今的相机镜头</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">也和萤石颇有渊源</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">因为硬度较低</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">很多珠宝商和矿物学者</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">不把萤石视作宝石范畴</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">然而萤石晶体形状规则</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">色泽晶莹剔透</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">实在不应被人忽视冷落</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">（摄影/冯欣艳）<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span border-box;\">更多的萤石或者细碎不成形</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">或者形成不见晶体的矿脉</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">聚集于矿山的岩石中</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">不具备美丽的结构和颜色</p><p powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">大洋深处有什么？</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">是无边无际的黑暗</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">还是生命止步的空寂？ </p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">你是否可以想象</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在大洋深处还隐藏着一个奇丽的世界</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">那里有巍巍的高山</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">有幽深的峡谷</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">有间歇喷发的“温泉”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">还有缤纷绚丽的“玫瑰花园”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">……</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">自古以来</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">人类就知道陆地上有山脉</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">到20世纪50年代初期</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">科学家们已经知道地球上</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">每个大洋的洋底都有“山脉”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这些“山脉”还连成了一个巨大的</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">海底“山脉系统”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">科学家将其命名为大洋中脊<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其相对高度为2000-3000米左右</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">绵延约8万公里</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">宽数百至数千公里</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其面积约占世界大洋总面积的33%</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">可与全球大陆面积相比</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(199, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;\">﹀</span></strong></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"311\" data-ratio=\"0.515625\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; width: 578px; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO4IkjnAZk5P47esegJKgTCGMoABGdBzOolHgjLBDaQ5lTlvMibovGlIN22X8f07w4cjsrcD6icak8ww/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">虽然同为巨大的山脉</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">但是大洋中脊和陆地山脉的生成机制不同</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">陆地山脉大多是由于板块相互挤压形成</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而大洋中脊则是新的大洋底部地壳</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">——洋壳生成的地方</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在大洋中脊的中轴线上</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">坐落着众多的“火山口”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在那里</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">灼热的岩浆由地幔上涌</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">然后逐渐冷却</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">结合周围的岩石形成了新的洋壳</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">中轴线处的洋壳由于刚刚形成</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">温度高，密度小</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">所以升得最高</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">形成了大洋中脊的峰线</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">然后</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在几百万年的地质时间尺度上</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">新洋壳从中轴线处不断往外扩张</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">温度逐渐降低</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">密度增加，慢慢下沉</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">于是，大洋中脊形成了<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(199, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;\">﹀</span></strong></p></section><section 56);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">③</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">鱼鳞云到底是什么云?</strong></p></section></section><section style=\"border-right: 2px solid rgb(199, 56, 56);margin-left: auto;border-bottom: 2px solid rgb(199, 56, 56);width: 12px;height: 12px;border-top-color: rgb(199, 56, 56);border-left-color: rgb(199, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">中国各地都有不少关于鱼鳞天的顺口溜</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而且大多和气象相关</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">“云势若鱼鳞，来日风不轻”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">“鱼鳞天，不过三”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">（不过三天就要刮风下雨）</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">“天上鲤鱼斑，晒谷不用翻”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">“瓦块鱼鳞珍珠云，太阳热得晒死人”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这些谚语说得花里胡哨</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其实无非在说两件事：</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">天上出现鱼鳞般的云彩</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">要么刮风下雨</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">要么天就一直晴好下去</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">同为鱼鳞云</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">为何却预示着两种截然相反的天气？</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其实，鱼鳞云有两种</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在高压控制下</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">特别是从冷高压转变为暖高压时</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">本地的空气稳定抬升</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">由于没有强烈对流</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">不会出现大朵的棉絮状云彩</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而是大范围水汽稳定抬升</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在高空冷凝形成范围很大的、</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">边界清晰的粗鱼鳞状云彩</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这也预示着天气将晴好下去</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(199, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">﹀</strong></span></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"381\" data-ratio=\"0.6578125\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; width: 578px; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO4IkjnAZk5P47esegJKgTCGGLvVE9iaamOGcgAMtU4Sh8skmQabddkOMsSYEiaox90M4icxPpyQQHy2g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"358\" data-ratio=\"0.61875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; width: 578px; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/g55FlNiaVwO4IkjnAZk5P47esegJKgTCGo68ZQibuGo3phV1afoZylIklNmELd6l61YtYCthgSWq3iaOhUhlgqfTw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">若天空中出现大面积密布的卷积云</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">说明有很强的扰动或者空气抬升作用</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">从而把空气中的水汽输送到高空大气层中</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这种情况一般说明距离本地不远的地方</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">有强的气旋或锋面的作用</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">同时，卷积云的存在</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">说明高空大气不稳定</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这种不稳定会从上至下影响中层</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">甚至低层的大气</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">使整个空气都变得不稳定</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这样一来，随着时间的推移</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">距离本地不远的气旋或锋面靠近</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">加之大气不稳定</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">共同作用的结果就是</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">天气转坏，风雨随之影响本地</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(199, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;\">﹀</span></strong></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">我们平时看到的彩虹</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">位置或高或低</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其实都只是彩虹的一部分</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">当太阳位于地平线时</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">彩虹形状如半圆</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">太阳的位置越高</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">彩虹的位置就越低</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如果太阳高度角大于42°</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">彩虹则出现在地平线之下</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">人在地面上就看不到了</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这也是为什么在中午难以见到彩虹的原因</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(199, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;\">﹀</span></strong></p></section><section style=\"text-align: border-box;\">在主虹的外侧</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如果运气好的话可以看到第二道彩虹</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">它被称作“副虹”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">也就是人们所说的“霓”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其色彩要比虹暗淡许多</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">古人形容华美衣服有一个词汇叫做“霓裳”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">霓没有虹艳丽</p><p style=\"box-sizing: powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">人为什么会有高山反应？</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这还要从大气压讲起</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">地球穿着一件厚厚的、</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">有分量的外衣——大气层</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">海拔越高，空气越稀薄</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">50%的大气</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">集中在海拔5500米高度以下</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">23%分布在海拔5500-10000米</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">15%分布在10000-15000米</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">海拔越高，人体血氧饱和度越低</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这被称为“低氧血症”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">也就是通常说的高原缺氧</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而人类就像鱼儿离不开水一样离不开氧</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(199, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;\">﹀</span></strong></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5171875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box;\">通常，进入高原2-3天后</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">出现反应的可能性最大</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">许多高山病症如高山肺水肿、脑水肿</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">也不能依靠吸氧即刻缓解</p><p border-box;\">“欺胖不欺瘦”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">“欺高不欺矮”</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">“欺动不欺静”等现象<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">格尔木烈士陵园的墓碑</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">记载了为了修筑青藏公路</p><p style=\"box-sizing: 255);border-right-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);border-left-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);margin-left: -5px;margin-right: -5px;padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">百年湘西，美酒传文化</strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">文化铸酒魂</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 0px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;border-right: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 3px solid transparent;border-bottom: 3px solid transparent;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.5px;padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;\">得天独厚的生态环境是酒鬼酒的品质保证，也是品牌的核心价值。</span></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;\">酒鬼酒产地湖南湘西，处于北纬30度世界酿酒黄金带。这里武陵迤逦，巍峨奇峻，沅醴交汇，百河汇湘，同时是众多世界遗产、国家风景名胜及自然保护区荟萃之地。不可复制的地理位置、厚重的历史渊源，为馥郁香型酒鬼酒赋予了别具一格的品牌内涵。独特的生态环境是酒鬼酒品质的强大保证，也是发展馥郁香型白酒产业的强大基础。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(180, 19, 19);box-sizing: border-box;\">如果说独特生态、匠心工艺是酒鬼酒的发展根基，那么湘西文化则赋予了酒鬼酒以“灵魂”。</span></strong></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.5px;padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;\">湖南省委宣传部常务副部长蒋祖烜，对于“沈从文先生笔下的湘西百年变迁”摄影和图书出版活动致辞表示：期待大家一起见证从沈从文笔下这一百年来湘西的变化、湖南的变化和中国的变化。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;width: 100%;border-width: 4px;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 3.2px 3.2px 8px;display: style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">△湖南省摄影家协会主席谢子龙</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;width: 100%;border-width: data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/g55FlNiaVwO6Nia1pTAXqP65wV2aP78b8gf4ric0L2ibaY09o74ic0ZTq0v814bxnwr45ljtenUhcFib3Vt2wPJb7ckg/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">△国际时尚摄影师及视觉艺术家陈漫</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.5px;padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;\">随后，湖南省摄影家协会主席谢子龙，天下凤凰文化传播公司董事长叶文智，国际时尚摄影师及视觉艺术家陈漫，著名学者、教授、博导、沈从文研究专家凌宇四位嘉宾大咖，分别作主题演讲，从湘西地域文化、湘西影像、沈从文文学研究三大方面分享与白酒、酒鬼酒的渊源。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;width: 100%;border-width: 4px;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 3.2px 3.2px 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/g55FlNiaVwO6Nia1pTAXqP65wV2aP78b8g4OOCpGosrtKGnCF9d5h2pwUsYlyfOWrJFwBp2vLVO6cN5dxBDaa2cA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">△著名学者、教授、博导、沈从文</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">研究专家凌宇作主题发言</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.5px;padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">《边城》是20世纪经典文学之作。《边城》结尾叙述翠翠独自守候在渡口，等待二佬的归来，“这个人也许永远不回来了，也许明天回来”。这是沈从文对湘西历史文化守望的象征性意象。凌宇教授从哲学思辨角度，向与会嘉宾分享沈从文对生命的理解。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(180, 19, 19);box-sizing: border-box;\">生活和生命，这两个概念，是沈从文生命中的两个基本范畴。</span></strong>生活，是人生存下来所必需的，衣食住行以及生儿育女；生命，是除了基本生活需要之外，人生的独立与自由、个人自我价值的实现。人不能只有生活而无生命，否则和动物无异。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/g55FlNiaVwO6Nia1pTAXqP65wV2aP78b8gmZgazTcxhg2Mh2esgIXQQNnE3Uia3kxSacHYcfXkpskqSwldxMQnMibQ/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">△著名书法家苏涛现场为酒鬼酒题词</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.5px;padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(180, 19, 19);box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">无疆，是一种人生阔境；有界，是一种智者大成。不可不醉，不可太醉，亦乎“无疆有界”。</strong></span><span style=\"color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;\">在滴滴美酒中融汇进湘西文化，独特的湘西风情将为酒鬼酒名扬世界锦上添花，相信酒鬼酒与《中国国家地理》的战略合作必将绽放不一样的跨界火花，创造别样的境界佳作，让我们拭目以待！</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p
